ุฒูุฑุงุก ููุฑูู ูุฒุฏุงุฏ ุงุญูุฑุงุฑุง ูุฑุฉ ุชูู ุงูุงุฎุฑู ููุงูุช ุญุฑูุฉ ูุงูุณ ูุงูููุณ ุจุญููููุง ุงูุงู ูุฐุง ุงูุฌูุน ุงูุบููุฑ ุงููุดุฉ ุงูุชู ูุตูุช ูุณููุน (ุงูู ุงุฎูุงูู ูุง ุณูุฏ ุชุงุฌุฑ ุงููุณ ูู ุงูุงุฏุจ ุงู ุชุณุงู ุงูุงูุณุฉ ูุจู ุญูููุงุ ูุงูุง ุงูุถุง ูุง ุณูุฏ ูุฑูุซ ุงูุฏูููุฉ! ููู ุชุฌุฑุค ุงูุชู ุชุดุชุนู ุบุถุจุง (ุงูุฏุฆู ูุง ูุฑูู ูุง ุจุฃุณ ุจูุฐุง ุงููุฏุฑ ููุง ุงู ุงูููุฉ ูุงุจุฏ ุงููุง ูู ุชูู ุงูุงุณุงุกุฉ) ุชููุฏุช ูุฑูู ูู ูุง ุชุฑูุฏ ุงู ุงูุงุฌูุงุก ุงูุฏุงูุฆุฉ ูุงูุนููู ุงูุชู ุชูุธุฑ ุงูู ุงููุชุงุชูู ูุงูุช ุฌูููุฉ ุฌุฏุง ุจุฏุง ุงู ุงูููุณ ููุงูุณ ูุฏ ุญุตูุง ุงุฎูุฑุง ุนูู ูุตูุจููุง ูู ุงูุญุจ ุงูุงุซูุงู ุงูุฐูู ูุฏ ุฒุงุฏุช ุงูุฑูุงูุงุช ุนูู ูููููุง ูู ููุนุง ูู ุงูุญุจ ุงุจุฏุง ูุฏ ุฌุนูุง ุงููุซูุฑ ูู ุงููุงุณ ูุฎุณุฑูู ุงููุงูุง ุทุงุฆูุฉ ุชูุฏู ูุงูุณ ุงูุฐู ูู ุงูููุฏู ููุงู ููู ููุณู ูุฏ ูุฑูู ุงูุชู ูู ุชุฑูุถ (ุณูุฏุงุชู ูุณุงุฏุชู ุงูุง ุจุงุดุฏ ุงูุณุนุงุฏุฉ ูุงูุณุฑูุฑ ูุงุนูู ุงู ูุฐู ุงููุณุงุจูุฉ ูุฏ ุงูุชูุช ุงูุงู! ููุฏ ูุงูุช ุงููุชูุฌุฉ ูุซุงููุฉ ุดูุฑุง ูุฌููุน ุงููุดุงุฑูุงุช ูุณูุชู ุชุนููุถ ุงูุฌููุน ุนู ุงููุงู ุงููุณุงุจูุฉ ูู ููุชุตููุง) ุงุนุชูุช ุตูุญุงุช ุงูุณุนุงุฏุฉ ุฌููุน ุงูุฐูู ุญุถุฑูุง ุงูู ูุฐุง ุงูููุฑุฌุงู ูุงู ูุฑูุญูู ุจูุฐู ุงููุชูุฌุฉ ุงููุซุงููุฉ ูุจุนุฏ ุงูููุฑุฌุงู ุบุฏุช ุงูุงุดุงุนุงุช ุนูู ุชูุชุณุญ ูู ููุงู ุญุชู ุงููุง ูุตูุช ุงูู ุงูุนุงุตูุฉ ูุงุตุจุญ ุงูููุฑุฌุงู ุงูุฐู ูุงู ูู ุงูููุชุฑุถ ุงู ูููู ุญุฏุซุง ุฏูููุง ุจุณูุทุง ุนูู ูุณุงู ุฌููุน ุณูุงู ุงูููููุฉ ูู ุงูุงุตููุง ุงูู ุงุทุฑุงููุง 

`,
                questions: [
                    "ูุง ุงูููุงูุฉ ุงูุชู ุชุชุฎูููุง ููุฐู ุงููุตุฉุ",
                    "ูู ุชุนุชูุฏ ุฃู ุจุนุถ ุงููุตุต ุฃูุถู ุจุฏูู ููุงูุฉ ูุญุฏุฏุฉุ"
                ]
            }
        ];

        // ูุธุงู ุงูุซููุงุช
        function setTheme(themeClass, storyTitle = '') {
            document.body.className = themeClass;
            const themeNames = {
                'theme-romance': 'ุฑููุงูุณู ๐',
                'theme-drama': 'ุฏุฑุงูู ๐ญ', 
                'theme-mystery': 'ุบุงูุถ ๐ต๏ธ',
                'theme-suspense': 'ุชุดูููู ๐'
            };
            
            const indicator = document.getElementById('themeIndicator');
            if (storyTitle) {
                indicator.textContent = `ุซูู ${themeNames[themeClass]} - ${storyTitle}`;
            } else {
                indicator.textContent = '';
            }
        }

        // ูุธุงู ุชุฎุฒูู ุงูุฃุฌูุจุฉ ูุงููุงููุงุช
        function getStoryAnswers(storyId) {
            const saved = localStorage.getItem(`story_${storyId}_answers`);
            return saved ? JSON.parse(saved) : [];
        }

        function saveStoryAnswer(storyId, questionIndex, answer) {
            const answers = getStoryAnswers(storyId);
            const newAnswer = {
                id: Date.now(),
                text: answer,
                questionIndex: questionIndex,
                timestamp: new Date().toLocaleString('ar-SA'),
                storyId: storyId,
                likes: 0,
                likedBy: []
            };
            
            answers.push(newAnswer);
            localStorage.setItem(`story_${storyId}_answers`, JSON.stringify(answers));
            return newAnswer;
        }

        function toggleLike(answerId, storyId) {
            const answers = getStoryAnswers(storyId);
            const answerIndex = answers.findIndex(a => a.id === answerId);
            
            if (answerIndex === -1) return false;

            const userLikes = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('user_likes') || '{}');
            const hasLiked = userLikes[answerId];

            if (hasLiked) {
                answers[answerIndex].likes--;
                answers[answerIndex].likedBy = answers[answerIndex].likedBy.filter(id => id !== 'user');
                delete userLikes[answerId];
            } else {
                answers[answerIndex].likes++;
                answers[answerIndex].likedBy.push('user');
                userLikes[answerId] = true;
            }

            localStorage.setItem(`story_${storyId}_answers`, JSON.stringify(answers));
            localStorage.setItem('user_likes', JSON.stringify(userLikes));
            return !hasLiked;
        }

        function displayStoryAnswers(storyId) {
            const answers = getStoryAnswers(storyId);
            const answersContainer = document.getElementById('answersContainer');
            const userLikes = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('user_likes') || '{}');
            
            answersContainer.innerHTML = '<h3>๐ฌ ุฃุฌูุจุฉ ุงููุฑุงุก:</h3>';
            
            if (answers.length === 0) {
                answersContainer.innerHTML += `
                    <div class="no-answers">
                        ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ุฃุฌูุจุฉ ุจุนุฏ... ูู ุฃูู ูู ูุดุงุฑู ุฑุฃูู!
                    </div>
                `;
                return;
            }

            const answersByQuestion = {};
            answers.forEach(answer => {
                if (!answersByQuestion[answer.questionIndex]) {
                    answersByQuestion[answer.questionIndex] = [];
                }
                answersByQuestion[answer.questionIndex].push(answer);
            });

            Object.keys(answersByQuestion).forEach(questionIndex => {
                const questionAnswers = answersByQuestion[questionIndex];
                
                answersContainer.innerHTML += `
                    <div class="question-answers">
                        <h4>๐ ุงูุณุคุงู ${parseInt(questionIndex) + 1}</h4>
                `;
                
                questionAnswers.forEach(answer => {
                    const isLiked = userLikes[answer.id];
                    answersContainer.innerHTML += `
                        <div class="answer-item">
                            <div class="answer-meta">
                                <span>โฐ ${answer.timestamp}</span>
                                <button class="like-btn ${isLiked ? 'liked' : ''}" 
                                        onclick="handleLike(${answer.id}, ${storyId})">
                                    <span class="likes-count">${answer.likes}</span> 
                                    ${isLiked ? 'โค๏ธ' : '๐ค'}
                                </button>
                            </div>
                            <p>${answer.text}</p>
                        </div>
                    `;
                });
                
                answersContainer.innerHTML += `</div>`;
            });
        }

        function handleLike(answerId, storyId) {
            const liked = toggleLike(answerId, storyId);
            displayStoryAnswers(storyId);
        }

        // Navigation Functions
        function showStories() {
            setTheme('', '');
            document.getElementById('storiesSection').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('storyReadingSection').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('questionsSection').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        function showStoryReading(storyId = null) {
            if (storyId) {
                const story = stories.find(s => s.id === storyId);
                document.getElementById('storyContent').innerHTML = 
                    `<h2>${story.title}</h2>
                     <div class="category">${story.category}</div>
                     <p>${story.content}</p>`;
                currentStoryId = storyId;
                
                // ุชุทุจูู ุซูู ุงููุตุฉ
                setTheme(story.theme, story.title);
                
                const progressBar = document.getElementById('readingProgress');
                progressBar.style.width = '0%';
                setTimeout(() => { progressBar.style.width = '100%'; }, 100);
            }
            
            document.getElementById('storiesSection').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('storyReadingSection').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('questionsSection').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        function showQuestions() {
            const story = stories.find(s => s.id === currentStoryId);
            const questionsContainer = document.getElementById('questionsContainer');
            questionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
            
            story.questions.forEach((question, index) => {
                questionsContainer.innerHTML += `
                    <div class="question">
                        <h3>${question}</h3>
                        <textarea placeholder="ุงูุชุจ ุฅุฌุงุจุชู ููุง..." id="answer${index}"></textarea>
                    </div>
                `;
            });
            
            questionsContainer.innerHTML += `
                <button class="submit-btn" onclick="submitAnswers()">ุฅุฑุณุงู ุงูุฅุฌุงุจุงุช</button>
            `;
            
            displayStoryAnswers(currentStoryId);
            
            document.getElementById('storyReadingSection').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('questionsSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        }

        function submitAnswers() {
            const story = stories.find(s => s.id === currentStoryId);
            const answersContainer = document.getElementById('answersContainer');
            
            let hasNewAnswers = false;
            story.questions.forEach((question, index) => {
                const answerInput = document.getElementById(`answer${index}`);
                if (answerInput && answerInput.value.trim()) {
                    saveStoryAnswer(currentStoryId, index, answerInput.value.trim());
                    answerInput.value = '';
                    hasNewAnswers = true;
                }
            });

            displayStoryAnswers(currentStoryId);

            if (hasNewAnswers) {
                const successMsg = document.createElement('div');
                successMsg.className = 'success-message';
                successMsg.textContent = 'โ ุชู ุญูุธ ุฅุฌุงุจุงุชู ุจูุฌุงุญ!';
                answersContainer.prepend(successMsg);

                setTimeout(() => {
                    successMsg.remove();
                }, 3000);
            }
        }

        // ุฅุญุตุงุฆูุงุช ุงูุฃุฌูุจุฉ
        function showAnswersStats() {
            const stats = {};
            stories.forEach(story => {
                const answers = getStoryAnswers(story.id);
                stats[story.title] = {
                    count: answers.length,
                    totalLikes: answers.reduce((sum, answer) => sum + answer.likes, 0)
                };
            });
            
            let statsHTML = '<h3>๐ ุฅุญุตุงุฆูุงุช ุงูุฃุฌูุจุฉ:</h3>';
            let totalAnswers = 0;
            let totalLikes = 0;
            
            Object.keys(stats).forEach(storyTitle => {
                totalAnswers += stats[storyTitle].count;
                totalLikes += stats[storyTitle].totalLikes;
                statsHTML += `
                    <div style="margin: 12px 0; padding: 15px; background: var(--secondary-color); border-radius: 10px; border-right: 4px solid var(--primary-color);">
                        <strong>${storyTitle}:</strong><br>
                        ๐ ${stats[storyTitle].count} ุฅุฌุงุจุฉ<br>
                        โค๏ธ ${stats[storyTitle].totalLikes} ูุงูู
                    </div>
                `;
            });
            
            statsHTML += `
                <div style="margin: 15px 0; padding: 15px; background: var(--primary-color); color: white; border-radius: 10px; text-align: center;">
                    <strong>ุงููุฌููุน:</strong><br>
                    ๐ ${totalAnswers} ุฅุฌุงุจุฉ<br>
                    โค๏ธ ${totalLikes} ูุงูู
                </div>
            `;
            
            alert(statsHTML);
        }

        // Initialize the page
        let currentStoryId = null;

        function initializePage() {
            // ุชุทุจูู ุงูุซูู ุงูุฃุณุงุณู
            setTheme('', '');
            
            // Generate story cards
            const storiesGrid = document.getElementById('storiesSection');
            storiesGrid.innerHTML = '';
            
            stories.forEach(story => {
                storiesGrid.innerHTML += `
                    <div class="story-card" onclick="showStoryReading(${story.id})">
                        <span class="category">${story.category}</span>
                        <h3>${story.title}</h3>
                        <p class="description">${story.description}</p>
                    </div>
                `;
            });
        }

        // Start the application
        initializePage();
    </script>
</body>
